```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

```dafny
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
```
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
```
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
```

  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0

  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }
  // At termination, i < 0 or s[i] != ')'.
  // Therefore, the suffix s[i+1 .. |s|) consists entirely of ')'.
  // Its length is |s| - (i+1) = |s| - i - 1,
  // and TrailingParens(s[..i+1]) = 0 because the prefix ends
  // with a non-')' character (or is empty).
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }
  // At loop exit, if i == -1 then the entire string consists of ')'.

  // Otherwise, i >= 0 and s[i] != ')', so TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0.
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
```

}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }

  // At this point, either i == -1 or s[i] != ')'.
  // If i == -1 (all characters were ')'), then
  //   TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == TrailingParens(s[..0]) == 0.
  // If i >= 0, we know s[i] != ')', so TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0.
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;

  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;

ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }
  // After the loop, i is either -1 or s[i] != ')'.
  // Therefore, the suffix s[i+1..] consists only of ')'.
  // The number of trailing ')' characters is |s| - (i+1).
  var trailing := |s| - (i + 1);
  var remaining := i + 1;
  assert TrailingParens(s) == trailing;
  bad := trailing > remaining;

```dafny
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0

}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
```

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{

}

  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
```

```dafny
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

Fix the assertions and return the complete program inside <DAFNY_CODE> tags.

ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }

```dafny
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
```

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

```dafny
// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }
  // At this point s[i+1 ..] (the suffix of trailing ')') has length |s| - (i+1)
  // and TrailingParens(s) equals that length.
  assert TrailingParens(s) == |s| - (i + 1);
  // The prefix up to i is non-empty or empty but contains no trailing ')'.
  // Hence TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0.
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
```

  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
```

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
```
